FNV PBR PPLIGHTING RESOURCE RESOLVER VTABLE AUDIT

Purpose:
1. Identify the object stored at renderer +0x8C4 that E7EA00 uses as a resource resolver.
2. Resolve candidate vtable slot +0x0C targets and decompile the selected slot methods.
3. Prove whether entry +8 resources become textures, render targets, persistent source textures, or non-material resources before visible PBR replacement.
